üî¢ Nimewo Antye (Integers) - Detay Konpl√®

üéØ Kisa se nimewo antye (Integer)?

Integer se nimewo antye ki pa gen pwen desimal. Yo ka pozitif, negatif, oswa zewo.

üí° TIP: Integer yo se nimewo konpl√® tankou 1, 2, 3, -5, 0. Yo pa gen pwen desimal.

üìã Karakteristik Integer

Karakteristik Deskripsyon Egzanp
Pozitif Nimewo plis 1, 25, 1000
Negatif Nimewo mwens -1, -25, -1000
Zewo Nimewo zewo 0
Gwo nimewo Nimewo ki gen anpil chif 1000000, 999999999

üîß Operasyon ak Integer

1. Operat√® Matematik Fondamantal:

# Egzanp nimewo antye
laj = 25
negatif = -10
zewo = 0
gwo_nimewo = 1000000

# Operasyon matematik
print("=== OPERASYON MATEMATIK ===")
print(f"Laj: {laj}")
print(f"Negatif: {negatif}")

# Adisyon
s√≤m = 5 + 3
print(f"5 + 3 = {s√≤m}")  # 8

# Soustraksyon
diferans = 10 - 4
print(f"10 - 4 = {diferans}")  # 6

# Miltiplikasyon
pwodui = 6 * 7
print(f"6 * 7 = {pwodui}")  # 42

# Divizyon (retounen float)
pwop√≤syon = 15 / 3
print(f"15 / 3 = {pwop√≤syon}")  # 5.0

# Divizyon anty√® (retounen integer)
divizyon_anty√® = 15 // 3
print(f"15 // 3 = {divizyon_anty√®}")  # 5

# R√®s divizyon (modulo)
r√®s = 17 % 5
print(f"17 % 5 = {r√®s}")  # 2

# Pisans
pisans = 2 ** 3
print(f"2 ** 3 = {pisans}")  # 8

2. Operat√® Konparezon:

# Konparezon integer
a = 10
b = 5

print("=== OPERAT√à KONPAREZON ===")
print(f"a = {a}, b = {b}")
print(f"a == b: {a == b}")  # False
print(f"a != b: {a != b}")  # True
print(f"a > b: {a > b}")    # True
print(f"a < b: {a < b}")    # False
print(f"a >= b: {a >= b}")  # True
print(f"a <= b: {a <= b}")  # False

3. Fonksyon Entegre ak Integer:

# Fonksyon entegre
lis_nimewo = [5, 2, 8, 1, 9]

print("=== FONKSYON ENTEGRE ===")
print(f"Lis: {lis_nimewo}")
print(f"Min: {min(lis_nimewo)}")  # 1
print(f"Max: {max(lis_nimewo)}")  # 9
print(f"Sum: {sum(lis_nimewo)}")  # 25
print(f"Abs(-5): {abs(-5)}")      # 5
print(f"Pow(2, 3): {pow(2, 3)}")  # 8
print(f"Round(3.7): {round(3.7)}") # 4

‚ö†Ô∏è Er√® Komen ak Integer

# ‚ùå ER√à KOMEN

# 1. Divize pa zewo
try:
    rezilta = 10 / 0
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("‚ùå Pa ka divize pa zewo!")

# 2. Konv√®ti string ki pa nimewo
try:
    nimewo = int("abc")
except ValueError:
    print("‚ùå 'abc' pa ka konv√®ti nan nimewo!")

# ‚úÖ SOLISYON S√àKIRITE

def divize_sekir(a, b):
    """Divize ak kontw√≤l er√®"""
    if b == 0:
        print("‚ö†Ô∏è Pa ka divize pa zewo!")
        return None
    return a / b

def konv√®ti_sekir(t√®ks):
    """Konv√®ti t√®ks nan nimewo ak kontw√≤l er√®"""
    try:
        return int(t√®ks)
    except ValueError:
        print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è '{t√®ks}' pa ka konv√®ti nan nimewo!")
        return None

# Teste fonksyon sekirite yo
print(divize_sekir(10, 2))    # 5.0
print(divize_sekir(10, 0))    # None
print(konv√®ti_sekir("123"))   # 123
print(konv√®ti_sekir("abc"))   # None

üéØ Float (Nimewo Desimal) - Detay Konpl√®

üéØ Kisa se Float?

Float se nimewo desimal ki gen pwen desimal. Yo reprezante nimewo rey√®l.

üí° TIP: Float yo se nimewo ki gen pwen desimal tankou 3.14, 2.5, -1.7.

üìã Karakteristik Float

Karakteristik Deskripsyon Egzanp
Pozitif Nimewo desimal plis 3.14, 2.5, 0.1
Negatif Nimewo desimal mwens -3.14, -2.5
Zewo Zewo desimal 0.0
Syantifik Nimewo ak eksponan 1e5 (100000), 2e-3 (0.002)

üîß Operasyon ak Float

# Egzanp float
pri = 25.99
pwa = 65.5
pi = 3.14159
negatif_float = -2.5

print("=== OPERASYON AK FLOAT ===")
print(f"Pri: {pri}")
print(f"Pwa: {pwa}")
print(f"Pi: {pi}")

# Operasyon matematik
kalkil = 3.14 + 2.86
print(f"3.14 + 2.86 = {kalkil}")  # 6.0

divizyon = 10 / 3
print(f"10 / 3 = {divizyon}")     # 3.3333333333333335

# Wonde
won_2 = round(3.14159, 2)
print(f"round(3.14159, 2) = {won_2}")  # 3.14

# Fonksyon matematik
import math
print(f"sqrt(16) = {math.sqrt(16)}")    # 4.0
print(f"ceil(3.2) = {math.ceil(3.2)}")  # 4
print(f"floor(3.8) = {math.floor(3.8)}") # 3

‚ö†Ô∏è ATANSYON: Float yo pa toujou presi 100%. Sa se n√≤mal nan pwogramasyon.

üî§ String (T√®ks) - Detay Konpl√®

üéØ Kisa se String?

String se kalite done pou t√®ks. Yo ka genyen l√®t, nimewo, espas, ak karakt√® espesyal.

üí° TIP: String yo se t√®ks tankou "Bonjou", "Marie", "123 ABC".

üìã Kreye String

# Fason diferan pou kreye string
string1 = "Bonjou"           # K√≤m doub
string2 = 'Mond'             # K√≤m s√®l
string3 = """Bonjou
Mond"""                      # String multiline
string4 = 'Li di: "Bonjou"'  # K√≤m nan string

print("=== KREYE STRING ===")
print(f"String 1: {string1}")
print(f"String 2: {string2}")
print(f"String 3: {string3}")
print(f"String 4: {string4}")

üîß String Slicing (Koupe ak Jwenn Pati)

Slicing p√®m√®t ou jwenn pati espesifik nan yon string.

# String pou egzanp
t√®ks = "Bonjou Mond"

print("=== STRING SLICING ===")
print(f"T√®ks konpl√®: '{t√®ks}'")
print(f"Long√®: {len(t√®ks)}")

# Aksede karakt√® endividy√®l
print(f"Premye karakt√®: '{t√®ks[0]}'")    # B
print(f"Dezy√®m karakt√®: '{t√®ks[1]}'")    # o
print(f"D√®nye karakt√®: '{t√®ks[-1]}'")    # d

# Slicing ak range
print(f"Pati 0-5: '{t√®ks[0:5]}'")       # Bonjo
print(f"Pati 6-11: '{t√®ks[6:11]}'")     # Mond
print(f"Pati 0-6: '{t√®ks[:6]}'")        # Bonjou
print(f"Pati 6-fin: '{t√®ks[6:]}'")      # Mond

# Slicing ak step
print(f"Chak 2 karakt√®: '{t√®ks[::2]}'") # Bno od
print(f"Ranv√®se: '{t√®ks[::-1]}'")       # dnoM uojnoB

üîß String Methods (Met√≤d String)

# String pou teste
t√®ks = "  Bonjou Mond  "

print("=== STRING METHODS ===")
print(f"T√®ks orijinal: '{t√®ks}'")

# Met√≤d fondamantal
print(f"Upper: '{t√®ks.upper()}'")        # BONJOU MOND
print(f"Lower: '{t√®ks.lower()}'")        # bonjou mond
print(f"Strip: '{t√®ks.strip()}'")        # Bonjou Mond
print(f"Capitalize: '{t√®ks.capitalize()}'") #   bonjou mond
print(f"Title: '{t√®ks.title()}'")        #   Bonjou Mond

# Met√≤d ch√®che
print(f"Find 'Mond': {t√®ks.find('Mond')}")  # 9
print(f"Count 'o': {t√®ks.count('o')}")      # 2
print(f"Startswith 'Bon': {t√®ks.startswith('Bon')}")  # False
print(f"Endswith 'd': {t√®ks.endswith('d')}")          # True

# Met√≤d modifye
print(f"Replace: '{t√®ks.replace('Mond', 'Ayiti')}'")  #   Bonjou Ayiti
print(f"Split: {t√®ks.split()}")                       # ['Bonjou', 'Mond']

üîß String Formatting (F√≤ma String)

# F√≤ma string ak f-strings (pi popil√®)
non = "Marie"
laj = 25
vil = "P√≤toprens"

print("=== STRING FORMATTING ===")

# F-string (rekomande)
mesaj1 = f"Bonjou {non}, ou gen {laj} ane, ou rete nan {vil}"
print(f"F-string: {mesaj1}")

# Format method
mesaj2 = "Bonjou {}, ou gen {} ane, ou rete nan {}".format(non, laj, vil)
print(f"Format method: {mesaj2}")

# Format ak index
mesaj3 = "Bonjou {0}, ou gen {1} ane, ou rete nan {2}".format(non, laj, vil)
print(f"Format ak index: {mesaj3}")

# Format ak non
mesaj4 = "Bonjou {nom}, ou gen {age} ane, ou rete nan {city}".format(nom=non, age=laj, city=vil)
print(f"Format ak non: {mesaj4}")

# Format nimewo
pri = 25.99
print(f"Pri: ${pri:.2f}")           # $25.99
print(f"Pousantaj: {0.75:.1%}")     # 75.0%
print(f"Nimewo: {1234:,}")          # 1,234

üîß String Concatenation (Konbine String)

# Konbine string yo
premye = "Bonjou"
dezy√®m = "Mond"

print("=== STRING CONCATENATION ===")

# Met√≤d 1: Operat√® +
konbine1 = premye + " " + dezy√®m
print(f"Operat√® +: {konbine1}")

# Met√≤d 2: join()
lis = [premye, dezy√®m]
konbine2 = " ".join(lis)
print(f"Join method: {konbine2}")

# Met√≤d 3: f-string
konbine3 = f"{premye} {dezy√®m}"
print(f"F-string: {konbine3}")

# Konbine plizy√® string
mo_yo = ["Bonjou", "tout", "moun", "nan", "Ayiti"]
fraz = " ".join(mo_yo)
print(f"Fraz konpl√®: {fraz}")

kantite = 100

temperati_fr√®t = -10 d√®t = -500 nivo_anba_mer = -1000

Operasyon ak nimewo antye

a = 10

diferans = a - b     # 7

# Multiplikasyon
pwodwi = a * b       # 30

# Divizyon (retounen float)

# Divizyon antye

# M√≤dilo (r√®s)

# Pisans
