import json
import csv
import argparse
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

class P√®son:
    """Klas paran pou El√®v ak Pwofes√®"""

    def __init__(self, non: str, laj: int, adr√®s: str = ""):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou P√®son

        Args:
            non (str): Non p√®son nan
            laj (int): Laj p√®son nan
            adr√®s (str): Adr√®s p√®son nan
        """
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        self.adr√®s = adr√®s
        self.dat_kreasyon = datetime.now().isoformat()

    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """Afiche enf√≤masyon p√®son nan"""
        print(f"üë§ Non: {self.non}")
        print(f"üéÇ Laj: {self.laj}")
        print(f"üè† Adr√®s: {self.adr√®s}")
        print(f"üìÖ Dat kreasyon: {self.dat_kreasyon}")

class El√®v(P√®son):
    """Klas El√®v ki herite nan P√®son"""

    def __init__(self, non: str, laj: int, klas: str, adr√®s: str = ""):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou El√®v

        Args:
            non (str): Non el√®v la
            laj (int): Laj el√®v la
            klas (str): Klas el√®v la
            adr√®s (str): Adr√®s el√®v la
        """
        super().__init__(non, laj, adr√®s)  # Rele konstrikt√® paran
        self.klas = klas
        self.n√≤t_yo = {}  # Diksyone: {maty√®: [n√≤t_yo]}
        self.matrik = self.jenere_matrik()

    def jenere_matrik(self) -> str:
        """Jenere nimewo matrik el√®v la"""
        ane = datetime.now().year
        # Senp: ane + 4 chif aleatwa
        import random
        chif_yo = random.randint(1000, 9999)
        return f"EL{ane}{chif_yo}"

    def ajoute_n√≤t(self, maty√®: str, n√≤t: float):
        """
        Ajoute yon n√≤t pou yon maty√®

        Args:
            maty√® (str): Non maty√® a
            n√≤t (float): N√≤t la (0-100)
        """
        if maty√® not in self.n√≤t_yo:
            self.n√≤t_yo[maty√®] = []

        if 0 <= n√≤t <= 100:
            self.n√≤t_yo[maty√®].append(n√≤t)
            print(f"‚úÖ N√≤t {n√≤t} ajoute pou {maty√®}")
        else:
            print("‚ùå N√≤t la dwe ant 0 ak 100")

    def kalkile_mway√®n(self, maty√®: str = None) -> float:
        """
        Kalkile mway√®n pou yon maty√® oswa tout maty√®

        Args:
            maty√® (str, optional): Maty√® espesifik. Defaults to None.

        Returns:
            float: Mway√®n la
        """
        if maty√®:
            if maty√® in self.n√≤t_yo and self.n√≤t_yo[maty√®]:
                return sum(self.n√≤t_yo[maty√®]) / len(self.n√≤t_yo[maty√®])
            return 0.0
        else:
            # Mway√®n jeneral
            tout_n√≤t = []
            for n√≤t_list in self.n√≤t_yo.values():
                tout_n√≤t.extend(n√≤t_list)

            if tout_n√≤t:
                return sum(tout_n√≤t) / len(tout_n√≤t)
            return 0.0

    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """Afiche enf√≤masyon el√®v la"""
        print(f"\nüéì EL√àV: {self.non}")
        print(f"üéÇ Laj: {self.laj}")
        print(f"üè´ Klas: {self.klas}")
        print(f"üìã Matrik: {self.matrik}")
        print(f"üè† Adr√®s: {self.adr√®s}")

        if self.n√≤t_yo:
            print("\nüìä N√íT YO:")
            for maty√®, n√≤t_list in self.n√≤t_yo.items():
                mway√®n = self.kalkile_mway√®n(maty√®)
                print(f"   üìö {maty√®}: {n√≤t_list} (Mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f})")

            mway√®n_jeneral = self.kalkile_mway√®n()
            print(f"\nüìà Mway√®n Jeneral: {mway√®n_jeneral:.2f}")
        else:
            print("üìä Pa gen n√≤t ank√≤")

class Pwofes√®(P√®son):
    """Klas Pwofes√® ki herite nan P√®son"""

    def __init__(self, non: str, laj: int, maty√®: str, sal√®: float, adr√®s: str = ""):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Pwofes√®

        Args:
            non (str): Non pwofes√® a
            laj (int): Laj pwofes√® a
            maty√® (str): Maty√® pwofes√® a anseye
            sal√® (float): Sal√® pwofes√® a
            adr√®s (str): Adr√®s pwofes√® a
        """
        super().__init__(non, laj, adr√®s)
        self.maty√® = maty√®
        self.sal√® = sal√®
        self.klas_yo = []  # Lis klas ke pwofes√® a anseye

    def ajoute_klas(self, klas: str):
        """Ajoute yon klas pou pwofes√® a"""
        if klas not in self.klas_yo:
            self.klas_yo.append(klas)
            print(f"‚úÖ Klas {klas} ajoute pou {self.non}")
        else:
            print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è Klas {klas} egziste deja")

    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """Afiche enf√≤masyon pwofes√® a"""
        print(f"\nüë®‚Äçüè´ PWOFES√à: {self.non}")
        print(f"üéÇ Laj: {self.laj}")
        print(f"üìö Maty√®: {self.maty√®}")
        print(f"üí∞ Sal√®: {self.sal√®} goud")
        print(f"üè† Adr√®s: {self.adr√®s}")
        print(f"üè´ Klas yo: {', '.join(self.klas_yo) if self.klas_yo else 'Pa gen klas ank√≤'}")

class Sist√®mJesyonLek√≤l:
    """Klas prensipal pou jere sist√®m lek√≤l la"""

    def __init__(self):
        """Konstrikt√® pou Sist√®mJesyonLek√≤l"""
        self.el√®v_yo = {}  # {non: El√®v}
        self.pwofes√®_yo = {}  # {non: Pwofes√®}
        self.fichier_el√®v = "el√®v_yo.json"
        self.fichier_pwofes√® = "pwofes√®_yo.json"
        self.chaje_done()

    def chaje_done(self):
        """Chaje done yo nan fichier yo"""
        try:
            # Chaje el√®v yo
            with open(self.fichier_el√®v, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                done_el√®v = json.load(f)
                for non, done in done_el√®v.items():
                    el√®v = El√®v(done['non'], done['laj'], done['klas'], done['adr√®s'])
                    el√®v.matrik = done['matrik']
                    el√®v.n√≤t_yo = done['n√≤t_yo']
                    self.el√®v_yo[non] = el√®v

            # Chaje pwofes√® yo
            with open(self.fichier_pwofes√®, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                done_pwofes√® = json.load(f)
                for non, done in done_pwofes√®.items():
                    pwofes√® = Pwofes√®(done['non'], done['laj'], done['maty√®'], done['sal√®'], done['adr√®s'])
                    pwofes√®.klas_yo = done['klas_yo']
                    self.pwofes√®_yo[non] = pwofes√®

            print("‚úÖ Done chaje ak siks√®")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("üìÅ Pa gen fichier done ank√≤")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"‚ùå Er√® nan chaje done: {e}")

    def sove_done(self):
        """Sove done yo nan fichier yo"""
        try:
            # Sove el√®v yo
            done_el√®v = {}
            for non, el√®v in self.el√®v_yo.items():
                done_el√®v[non] = {
                    'non': el√®v.non,
                    'laj': el√®v.laj,
                    'klas': el√®v.klas,
                    'adr√®s': el√®v.adr√®s,
                    'matrik': el√®v.matrik,
                    'n√≤t_yo': el√®v.n√≤t_yo,
                    'dat_kreasyon': el√®v.dat_kreasyon
                }

            with open(self.fichier_el√®v, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(done_el√®v, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

            # Sove pwofes√® yo
            done_pwofes√® = {}
            for non, pwofes√® in self.pwofes√®_yo.items():
                done_pwofes√®[non] = {
                    'non': pwofes√®.non,
                    'laj': pwofes√®.laj,
                    'maty√®': pwofes√®.maty√®,
                    'sal√®': pwofes√®.sal√®,
                    'adr√®s': pwofes√®.adr√®s,
                    'klas_yo': pwofes√®.klas_yo,
                    'dat_kreasyon': pwofes√®.dat_kreasyon
                }

            with open(self.fichier_pwofes√®, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(done_pwofes√®, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

            print("‚úÖ Done sove ak siks√®")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"‚ùå Er√® nan sove done: {e}")

    # === JESYON EL√àV ===

    def ajoute_el√®v(self, non: str, laj: int, klas: str, adr√®s: str = ""):
        """Ajoute yon nouvo el√®v"""
        if non in self.el√®v_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå El√®v {non} egziste deja")
            return False

        el√®v = El√®v(non, laj, klas, adr√®s)
        self.el√®v_yo[non] = el√®v
        print(f"‚úÖ El√®v {non} ajoute ak siks√®")
        return True

    def modifye_el√®v(self, non: str, laj: int = None, klas: str = None, adr√®s: str = None):
        """Modifye enf√≤masyon yon el√®v"""
        if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå El√®v {non} pa jwenn")
            return False

        el√®v = self.el√®v_yo[non]
        if laj is not None:
            el√®v.laj = laj
        if klas is not None:
            el√®v.klas = klas
        if adr√®s is not None:
            el√®v.adr√®s = adr√®s

        print(f"‚úÖ Enf√≤masyon el√®v {non} modifye")
        return True

    def efase_el√®v(self, non: str):
        """Efase yon el√®v"""
        if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå El√®v {non} pa jwenn")
            return False

        del self.el√®v_yo[non]
        print(f"‚úÖ El√®v {non} efase")
        return True

    # === JESYON PWOFES√à ===

    def ajoute_pwofes√®(self, non: str, laj: int, maty√®: str, sal√®: float, adr√®s: str = ""):
        """Ajoute yon nouvo pwofes√®"""
        if non in self.pwofes√®_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå Pwofes√® {non} egziste deja")
            return False

        pwofes√® = Pwofes√®(non, laj, maty√®, sal√®, adr√®s)
        self.pwofes√®_yo[non] = pwofes√®
        print(f"‚úÖ Pwofes√® {non} ajoute ak siks√®")
        return True

    def modifye_pwofes√®(self, non: str, laj: int = None, maty√®: str = None, sal√®: float = None, adr√®s: str = None):
        """Modifye enf√≤masyon yon pwofes√®"""
        if non not in self.pwofes√®_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå Pwofes√® {non} pa jwenn")
            return False

        pwofes√® = self.pwofes√®_yo[non]
        if laj is not None:
            pwofes√®.laj = laj
        if maty√® is not None:
            pwofes√®.maty√® = maty√®
        if sal√® is not None:
            pwofes√®.sal√® = sal√®
        if adr√®s is not None:
            pwofes√®.adr√®s = adr√®s

        print(f"‚úÖ Enf√≤masyon pwofes√® {non} modifye")
        return True

    def efase_pwofes√®(self, non: str):
        """Efase yon pwofes√®"""
        if non not in self.pwofes√®_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå Pwofes√® {non} pa jwenn")
            return False

        del self.pwofes√®_yo[non]
        print(f"‚úÖ Pwofes√® {non} efase")
        return True

    # === JESYON N√íT ===

    def ajoute_n√≤t_el√®v(self, non_el√®v: str, maty√®: str, n√≤t: float):
        """Ajoute yon n√≤t pou yon el√®v"""
        if non_el√®v not in self.el√®v_yo:
            print(f"‚ùå El√®v {non_el√®v} pa jwenn")
            return False

        self.el√®v_yo[non_el√®v].ajoute_n√≤t(maty√®, n√≤t)
        return True

    # === RAP√í AK ESTATISTIK ===

    def rap√≤_el√®v_yo(self):
        """Afiche rap√≤ sou tout el√®v yo"""
        print("\nüìä RAP√í EL√àV YO")
        print("=" * 40)

        if not self.el√®v_yo:
            print("üìù Pa gen el√®v ank√≤")
            return

        for non, el√®v in self.el√®v_yo.items():
            el√®v.afiche_inf√≤()
            print("-" * 40)

    def rap√≤_pwofes√®_yo(self):
        """Afiche rap√≤ sou tout pwofes√® yo"""
        print("\nüë®‚Äçüè´ RAP√í PWOFES√à YO")
        print("=" * 40)

        if not self.pwofes√®_yo:
            print("üìù Pa gen pwofes√® ank√≤")
            return

        for non, pwofes√® in self.pwofes√®_yo.items():
            pwofes√®.afiche_inf√≤()
            print("-" * 40)

    def estatistik_lek√≤l(self):
        """Afiche estatistik lek√≤l la"""
        print("\nüìà ESTATISTIK LEK√íL LA")
        print("=" * 40)

        total_el√®v = len(self.el√®v_yo)
        total_pwofes√® = len(self.pwofes√®_yo)

        print(f"üéì Total el√®v: {total_el√®v}")
        print(f"üë®‚Äçüè´ Total pwofes√®: {total_pwofes√®}")

        if total_el√®v > 0:
            # Estatistik el√®v yo
            klas_yo = {}
            mway√®n_yo = []

            for el√®v in self.el√®v_yo.values():
                # Konte el√®v pa klas
                if el√®v.klas not in klas_yo:
                    klas_yo[el√®v.klas] = 0
                klas_yo[el√®v.klas] += 1

                # Kolekte mway√®n yo
                mway√®n = el√®v.kalkile_mway√®n()
                if mway√®n > 0:
                    mway√®n_yo.append(mway√®n)

            print(f"\nüìö El√®v pa klas:")
            for klas, kantite in klas_yo.items():
                print(f"   {klas}: {kantite} el√®v")

            if mway√®n_yo:
                mway√®n_jeneral = sum(mway√®n_yo) / len(mway√®n_yo)
                print(f"\nüìä Mway√®n jeneral lek√≤l la: {mway√®n_jeneral:.2f}")

        if total_pwofes√® > 0:
            # Estatistik pwofes√® yo
            maty√®_yo = {}
            total_sal√® = 0

            for pwofes√® in self.pwofes√®_yo.values():
                if pwofes√®.maty√® not in maty√®_yo:
                    maty√®_yo[pwofes√®.maty√®] = 0
                maty√®_yo[pwofes√®.maty√®] += 1
                total_sal√® += pwofes√®.sal√®

            print(f"\nüìö Pwofes√® pa maty√®:")
            for maty√®, kantite in maty√®_yo.items():
                print(f"   {maty√®}: {kantite} pwofes√®")

            sal√®_mway√®n = total_sal√® / total_pwofes√®
            print(f"\nüí∞ Sal√® mway√®n: {sal√®_mway√®n:.2f} goud")

def main():
    """Fonksyon prensipal"""
    # Kreye sist√®m nan
    sist√®m = Sist√®mJesyonLek√≤l()

def ajoute_n√≤t(self, non, n√≤t):
    if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
        raise ValueError(f"El√®v {non} pa egziste")

    if not isinstance(n√≤t, (int, float)) or n√≤t < 0 or n√≤t > 20:
        raise ValueError("N√≤t dwe yon nimewo ant 0 ak 20")

    self.el√®v_yo[non]["n√≤t_yo"].append(n√≤t)
    print(f"N√≤t {n√≤t} ajoute pou {non}")

def kalkile_mway√®n(self, non):
    if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
        raise ValueError(f"El√®v {non} pa egziste")

    n√≤t_yo = self.el√®v_yo[non]["n√≤t_yo"]
    if not n√≤t_yo:
        return 0

    return sum(n√≤t_yo) / len(n√≤t_yo)

def jenera_rap√≤(self):
    print("\n=== RAP√í EL√àV YO ===")
    for non, enf√≤ in self.el√®v_yo.items():
        mway√®n = self.kalkile_mway√®n(non)
        print(f"{non}: {enf√≤['klas']}, Mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f}")

def sove_done(self):
    with open(self.fichier_done, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(self.el√®v_yo, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    print("Done sove ak siks√®")

def chaje_done(self):
    try:
        with open(self.fichier_done, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            self.el√®v_yo = json.load(f)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        self.el√®v_yo = {}

def eksp√≤t_csv(self, non_fichier):
    with open(non_fichier, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="") as f:
        ekriv√® = csv.writer(f)
        ekriv√®.writerow(["Non", "Laj", "Klas", "Mway√®n"])

        for non, enf√≤ in self.el√®v_yo.items():
            mway√®n = self.kalkile_mway√®n(non)
            ekriv√®.writerow([non, enf√≤["laj"], enf√≤["klas"], f"{mway√®n:.2f}"])

    print(f"Rap√≤ eksp√≤te nan {non_fichier}")
